1. Experiment Design
abbreviations for strains: AB: het; AA: hom
type of cross: Backcross
number of mice phenotyped: 312
total number of mice phenotypes: 2 [1 binary/1 quantiative]
phenotypes: diabetic status/group [binary] & age of onset [continuous]
number of mice: 312
number of markers: 137302
covariates: sex [F: 312; M: 0] (sex not used as all females); binary diabetic status for continous traits

2. Genotype QC

  • Step 1: Sample QC
  • Step 2: SNP QC(removing monomorphic, genotype error & missing markers)
  • Step 3: Preparing Files for QTL Analysis
  • Step 4: Identifying additional disproportionate markers within each sample set
    • ICI vs EOI
    • ICI vs PBS
    • ICI-Early vs PBS
    • ICI-Early vs PBS & ICI-Late outcome the same as ICI vs PBS

3. Phenotype QC

continous phenotypes (age of onset)

  • Corrected Phenotypes
    • ICI vs PBS & ICI-Early vs PBS & ICI vs EOI (EOI set as missing)
    • ICI-Early vs PBS & ICI-Late outcome the same as ICI vs PBS

4. QTL Analysis

binary phenotpe (diabetic status/group)

  1. removed additional low frequency markers as well as disproportionate markers (identified in Step 2.4) within each sample set
  2. no X covariate (ie. Xcovar)
  3. no kinship included as r/qtl2 does not allow for the inclusion of a kinship matrix in this type of model
  4. For each model run, permutations (1000) were used for each model to obtain genome-wide LOD significance threshold for p < 0.01, p < 0.05, p < 0.10, respectively, separately for X and automsomes (A)
  • ICI vs EOI

The following analysis has been done with age of onset as all samples have a value:

  • ICI vs PBS
    • no additional information about peaks
    • with additional information about peaks
  • ICI-Early vs PBS
  • ICI-Early vs PBS & ICI-Late

continous phenotypes (age of onset)

  1. removed additional low frequency markers as well as disproportionate markers (identified in Step 2.4) within each sample set
  2. disease status was used as a binary covariate (that is, diabetes/no diabetes or yes/no) for analyses in each sample set
  3. no X covariate (ie. Xcovar) 4 no kinship included
  4. For each model run, permutations (1000) were used for each model to obtain genome-wide LOD significance threshold for p < 0.01, p < 0.05, p < 0.10, respectively, separately for X and automsomes (A)

age of onset

  • ICI vs PBS
  • ICI-Early vs PBS
  • ICI-Early vs PBS & ICI-Late

age of onset (rank normalised)
